<s> BECKET AND OTHER PLAYS BY ALFRED LORD TENNYSON, POET LAUREATE CONTENTS BECKET THE CUP THE FALCON THE PROMISE OF MAY BECKET TO THE LORD CHANCELLOR, THE RIGHT HONOURABLE EARL OF SELBORNE </s>
<s> MY DEAR SELBORNE, _To you, the honoured Chancellor of our own day, I dedicate this dramatic memorial of your great predecessor;--which, altho' not intended in its present form to meet the exigencies of our modern theatre, has nevertheless--for so you have assured me--won your approbation </s>
<s> Ever yours_, TENNYSON </s>
<s> _DRAMATIS PERSONAE_ </s>
<s> HENRY II </s>
<s> (_son of the Earl of Anjou_) </s>
<s> THOMAS BECKET, _Chancellor of England, afterwards Archbishop of Canterbury_ </s>
<s> GILBERT FOLIOT, _Bishop of London_ </s>
<s> ROGER, _Archbishop of York_ </s>

<s> JOHN OF SALISBURY | HERBERT OF BOSHAM | _friends of Becket_ </s>
<s> WALTER MAP, _reputed author of 'Golias,' Latin poems against the priesthood_ </s>

<s> GEOFFREY, _son of Rosamund and Henry_ </s>

<s> PROLOGUE </s>
<s> _A Castle in Normandy </s>
<s> Interior of the Hall </s>
<s> Roofs of a City seen thro' Windows_ </s>
<s> HENRY _and_ BECKET _at chess_ </s>
<s> HENRY </s>
<s> So then our good Archbishop Theobald Lies dying </s>
<s> BECKET </s>
<s> I am grieved to know as much </s>
<s> HENRY </s>
<s> But we must have a mightier man than he For his successor </s>
<s> BECKET </s>
<s> Have you thought of one </s>
<s> HENRY </s>
<s> A cleric lately poison'd his own mother, And being brought before the courts of the Church, They but degraded him </s>
<s> I hope they whipt him </s>
<s> I would have hang'd him </s>
<s> BECKET </s>
<s> It is your move </s>
<s> HENRY </s>
<s> Well--there </s>
<s> [_Moves_ </s>
<s> The Church in the pell-mell of Stephen's time Hath climb'd the throne and almost clutch'd the crown; But by the royal customs of our realm The Church should hold her baronies of me, Like other lords amenable to law </s>
<s> I'll have them written down and made the law </s>
<s> BECKET </s>
<s> My liege, I move my bishop </s>
<s> HENRY </s>
<s> And if I live, No man without my leave shall excommunicate My tenants or my household </s>
<s> BECKET </s>
<s> Look to your king </s>
<s> HENRY </s>
<s> No man without my leave shall cross the seas To set the Pope against me--I pray your pardon </s>
<s> BECKET </s>
<s> Well--will you move </s>
<s> HENRY </s>
<s> There </s>
<s> [_Moves_ </s>
<s> BECKET </s>
<s> Check--you move so wildly </s>
<s> HENRY </s>
<s> There then </s>
<s> [_Moves_ </s>
<s> BECKET </s>
<s> Why--there then, for you see my bishop Hath brought your king to a standstill </s>
<s> You are beaten </s>
<s> HENRY (_kicks over the board_) </s>
<s> Why, there then--down go bishop and king together </s>
<s> I loathe being beaten; had I fixt my fancy Upon the game I should have beaten thee, But that was vagabond </s>
<s> BECKET </s>
<s> Where, my liege </s>
<s> With Phryne, Or Lais, or thy Rosamund, or another </s>
<s> HENRY </s>
<s> My Rosamund is no Lais, Thomas Becket; And yet she plagues me too--no fault in her-- But that I fear the Queen would have her life </s>
<s> BECKET </s>
<s> Put her away, put her away, my liege </s>
<s> Put her away into a nunnery </s>
<s> Safe enough there from her to whom thou art bound By Holy Church </s>
<s> And wherefore should she seek The life of Rosamund de Clifford more Than that of other paramours of thine </s>
<s> HENRY </s>
<s> How dost thou know I am not wedded to her </s>
<s> BECKET </s>
<s> How should I know </s>
<s> HENRY </s>
<s> That is my secret, Thomas </s>
<s> BECKET </s>
<s> State secrets should be patent to the statesman Who serves and loves his king, and whom the king Loves not as statesman, but true lover and friend </s>
<s> HENRY </s>
<s> Come, come, thou art but deacon, not yet bishop, No, nor archbishop, nor my confessor yet </s>
<s> I would to God thou wert, for I should find An easy father confessor in thee </s>
<s> BECKET </s>
<s> St </s>
<s> Denis, that thou shouldst not </s>
<s> I should beat Thy kingship as my bishop hath beaten it </s>
<s> HENRY </s>
<s> Hell take thy bishop then, and my kingship too </s>
<s> Come, come, I love thee and I know thee, I know thee, A doter on white pheasant-flesh at feasts, A sauce-deviser for thy days of fish, A dish-designer, and most amorous Of good old red sound liberal Gascon wine: Will not thy body rebel, man, if thou flatter it </s>
<s> BECKET </s>
<s> That palate is insane which cannot tell A good dish from a bad, new wine from old </s>
<s> HENRY </s>
<s> Well, who loves wine loves woman </s>
<s> BECKET </s>
<s> So I do </s>
<s> Men are God's trees, and women are God's flowers; And when the Gascon wine mounts to my head, The trees are all the statelier, and the flowers Are all the fairer </s>
<s> HENRY </s>
<s> And thy thoughts, thy fancies </s>
<s> BECKET </s>
<s> Good dogs, my liege, well train'd, and easily call'd Off from the game </s>
<s> HENRY </s>
<s> Save for some once or twice, When they ran down the game and worried it </s>
<s> BECKET </s>
<s> No, my liege, no!--not once--in God's name, no </s>
<s> HENRY </s>
<s> Nay, then, I take thee at thy word--believe thee The veriest Galahad of old Arthur's hall </s>
<s> And so this Rosamund, my true heart-wife, Not Eleanor--she whom I love indeed As a woman should be loved--Why dost thou smile So dolorously </s>
<s> BECKET </s>
<s> My good liege, if a man Wastes himself among women, how should he love A woman, as a woman should be loved </s>
<s> HENRY </s>
<s> How shouldst thou know that never hast loved one </s>
<s> Come, I would give her to thy care in England When I am out in Normandy or Anjou </s>
<s> BECKET </s>
<s> My lord, I am your subject, not your-- HENRY </s>
<s> Pander </s>
<s> God's eyes </s>
<s> I know all that--not my purveyor Of pleasures, but to save a life--her life; Ay, and the soul of Eleanor from hell-fire </s>
<s> I have built a secret bower in England, Thomas, A nest in a bush </s>
<s> BECKET </s>
<s> And where, my liege </s>
<s> HENRY (_whispers_) </s>
<s> Thine ear </s>
<s> BECKET </s>
<s> That's lone enough </s>
<s> HENRY (_laying paper on table_) </s>
<s> This chart here mark'd '_Her Bower_,' Take, keep it, friend </s>
<s> See, first, a circling wood, A hundred pathways running everyway, And then a brook, a bridge; and after that This labyrinthine brickwork maze in maze, And then another wood, and in the midst A garden and my Rosamund </s>
<s> Look, this line-- The rest you see is colour'd green--but this Draws thro' the chart to her </s>
<s> BECKET </s>
<s> This blood-red line </s>
<s> HENRY </s>
<s> Ay </s>
<s> blood, perchance, except thou see to her </s>
<s> BECKET </s>
<s> And where is she </s>
<s> There in her English nest </s>
<s> HENRY </s>
<s> Would God she were--no, here within the city </s>
<s> We take her from her secret bower in Anjou And pass her to her secret bower in England </s>
<s> She is ignorant of all but that I love her </s>
<s> BECKET </s>
<s> My liege, I pray thee let me hence: a widow And orphan child, whom one of thy wild barons-- HENRY </s>
<s> Ay, ay, but swear to see to her in England </s>
<s> BECKET </s>
<s> Well, well, I swear, but not to please myself </s>
<s> HENRY </s>
<s> Whatever come between us </s>
<s> BECKET </s>
<s> What should come Between us, Henry </s>
<s> HENRY </s>
<s> Nay--I know not, Thomas </s>
<s> BECKET </s>
<s> What need then </s>
<s> Well--whatever come between us </s>
<s> [_Going_ </s>
<s> HENRY </s>
<s> A moment </s>
<s> thou didst help me to my throne In Theobald's time, and after by thy wisdom Hast kept it firm from shaking; but now I, For my realm's sake, myself must be the wizard To raise that tempest which will set it trembling Only to base it deeper </s>
<s> I, true son Of Holy Church--no croucher to the Gregories That tread the kings their children underheel-- Must curb her; and the Holy Father, while This Barbarossa butts him from his chair, Will need my help--be facile to my hands </s>
<s> Now is my time </s>
<s> Yet--lest there should be flashes And fulminations from the side of Rome, An interdict on England--I will have My young son Henry crown'd the King of England, That so the Papal bolt may pass by England, As seeming his, not mine, and fall abroad </s>
<s> I'll have it done--and now </s>
<s> BECKET </s>
<s> Surely too young Even for this shadow of a crown; and tho' I love him heartily, I can spy already A strain of hard and headstrong in him </s>
<s> Say, The Queen should play his kingship against thine </s>
<s> HENRY </s>
<s> I will not think so, Thomas </s>
<s> Who shall crown him </s>
<s> Canterbury is dying </s>
<s> BECKET </s>
<s> The next Canterbury </s>
<s> HENRY </s>
<s> And who shall he be, my friend Thomas </s>
<s> Who </s>
<s> BECKET </s>
<s> Name him; the Holy Father will confirm him </s>
<s> HENRY (_lays his hand on_ BECKET'S _shoulder_) </s>
<s> Here </s>
<s> BECKET </s>
<s> Mock me not </s>
<s> I am not even a monk </s>
<s> Thy jest--no more </s>
<s> Why--look--is this a sleeve For an archbishop </s>
<s> HENRY </s>
<s> But the arm within Is Becket's, who hath beaten down my foes </s>
<s> BECKET </s>
<s> A soldier's, not a spiritual arm </s>
<s> HENRY </s>
<s> I lack a spiritual soldier, Thomas-- A man of this world and the next to boot </s>
<s> BECKET </s>
<s> There's Gilbert Foliot </s>
<s> HENRY </s>
<s> He </s>
<s> too thin, too thin </s>
<s> Thou art the man to fill out the Church robe; Your Foliot fasts and fawns too much for me </s>
<s> BECKET </s>
<s> Roger of York </s>
<s> HENRY </s>
<s> Roger is Roger of York </s>
<s> King, Church, and State to him but foils wherein To set that precious jewel, Roger of York </s>
<s> No </s>
<s> BECKET </s>
<s> Henry of Winchester </s>
<s> HENRY </s>
<s> Him who crown'd Stephen-- King Stephen's brother </s>
<s> No; too royal for me </s>
<s> And I'll have no more Anselms </s>
<s> BECKET </s>
<s> Sire, the business Of thy whole kingdom waits me: let me go </s>
<s> HENRY </s>
<s> Answer me first </s>
<s> BECKET </s>
<s> Then for thy barren jest Take thou mine answer in bare commonplace-- _Nolo episcopari_ </s>
<s> HENRY </s>
<s> Ay, but _Nolo Archiepiscopari_, my good friend, Is quite another matter </s>
<s> BECKET </s>
<s> A more awful one </s>
<s> Make _me_ archbishop </s>
<s> Why, my liege, I know Some three or four poor priests a thousand times Fitter for this grand function </s>
<s> _Me_ archbishop </s>
<s> God's favour and king's favour might so clash That thou and I----That were a jest indeed </s>
<s> HENRY </s>
<s> Thou angerest me, man: I do not jest </s>
<s> _Enter_ ELEANOR _and_ SIR REGINALD FITZURSE </s>
<s> ELEANOR (_singing_) </s>
<s> Over </s>
<s> the sweet summer closes, The reign of the roses is done-- HENRY (_to_ BECKET, _who is going_) </s>
<s> Thou shalt not go </s>
<s> I have not ended with thee </s>
<s> ELEANOR (_seeing chart on table_) </s>
<s> This chart with the red line </s>
<s> her bower </s>
<s> whose bower </s>
<s> HENRY </s>
<s> The chart is not mine, but Becket's: take it, Thomas </s>
<s> ELEANOR </s>
<s> Becket </s>
<s> O--ay--and these chessmen on the floor--the king's crown broken </s>
<s> Becket hath beaten thee again--and thou hast kicked down the board </s>
<s> I know thee of old </s>
<s> HENRY </s>
<s> True enough, my mind was set upon other matters </s>
<s> ELEANOR </s>
<s> What matters </s>
<s> State matters </s>
<s> love matters </s>
<s> HENRY </s>
<s> My love for thee, and thine for me </s>
<s> ELEANOR </s>
<s> Over </s>
<s> the sweet summer closes, The reign of the roses is done; Over and gone with the roses, And over and gone with the sun </s>
<s> Here; but our sun in Aquitaine lasts longer </s>
<s> I would I were in Aquitaine again--your north chills me </s>
<s> Over </s>
<s> the sweet summer closes, And never a flower at the close; Over and gone with the roses, And winter again and the snows </s>
<s> That was not the way I ended it first--but unsymmetrically, preposterously, illogically, out of passion, without art--like a song of the people </s>
<s> Will you have it </s>
<s> The last Parthian shaft of a forlorn Cupid at the King's left breast, and all left-handedness and under-handedness </s>
<s> And never a flower at the close, Over and gone with the roses, Not over and gone with the rose </s>
<s> True, one rose will outblossom the rest, one rose in a bower </s>
<s> I speak after my fancies, for I am a Troubadour, you know, and won the violet at Toulouse; but my voice is harsh here, not in tune, a nightingale out of season; for marriage, rose or no rose, has killed the golden violet </s>
<s> BECKET </s>
<s> Madam, you do ill to scorn wedded love </s>
<s> ELEANOR </s>
<s> So I do </s>
<s> Louis of France loved me, and I dreamed that I loved Louis of France: and I loved Henry of England, and Henry of England dreamed that he loved me; but the marriage-garland withers even with the putting on, the bright link rusts with the breath of the first after-marriage kiss, the harvest moon is the ripening of the harvest, and the honeymoon is the gall of love; he dies of his honeymoon </s>
<s> I could pity this poor world myself that it is no better ordered </s>
<s> HENRY </s>
<s> Dead is he, my Queen </s>
<s> What, altogether </s>
<s> Let me swear nay to that by this cross on thy neck </s>
<s> God's eyes </s>
<s> what a lovely cross </s>
<s> what jewels </s>
<s> ELEANOR </s>
<s> Doth it please you </s>
<s> Take it and wear it on that hard heart of yours-- there </s>
<s> [_Gives it to him_ </s>
<s> HENRY (_puts it on_) </s>
<s> On this left breast before so hard a heart, To hide the scar left by thy Parthian dart </s>
<s> ELEANOR </s>
<s> Has my simple song set you jingling </s>
<s> Nay, if I took and translated that hard heart into our Provençal facilities, I could so play about it with the rhyme-- HENRY </s>
<s> That the heart were lost in the rhyme and the matter in the metre </s>
<s> May we not pray you, Madam, to spare us the hardness of your facility </s>
<s> ELEANOR </s>
<s> The wells of Castaly are not wasted upon the desert </s>
<s> We did but jest </s>
<s> HENRY </s>
<s> There's no jest on the brows of Herbert there </s>
<s> What is it, Herbert </s>
<s> _Enter_ HERBERT OF BOSHAM </s>
<s> HERBERT </s>
<s> My liege, the good Archbishop is no more </s>
<s> HENRY </s>
<s> Peace to his soul </s>
<s> HERBERT </s>
<s> I left him with peace on his face--that sweet other-world smile, which will be reflected in the spiritual body among the angels </s>
<s> But he longed much to see your Grace and the Chancellor ere he past, and his last words were a commendation of Thomas Becket to your Grace as his successor in the archbishoprick </s>
<s> HENRY </s>
<s> Ha, Becket </s>
<s> thou rememberest our talk </s>
<s> BECKET </s>
<s> My heart is full of tears--I have no answer </s>
<s> HENRY </s>
<s> Well, well, old men must die, or the world would grow mouldy, would only breed the past again </s>
<s> Come to me to-morrow </s>
<s> Thou hast but to hold out thy hand </s>
<s> Meanwhile the revenues are mine </s>
<s> A-hawking, a-hawking </s>
<s> If I sit, I grow fat </s>
<s> [_Leaps over the table, and exit_ </s>
<s> BECKET </s>
<s> He did prefer me to the chancellorship, Believing I should ever aid the Church-- But have I done it </s>
<s> He commends me now From out his grave to this archbishoprick </s>
<s> HERBERT </s>
<s> A dead man's dying wish should be of weight </s>
<s> BECKET </s>
<s> _His_ should </s>
<s> Come with me </s>
<s> Let me learn at full The manner of his death, and all he said </s>
<s> [_Exeunt_ HERBERT _and_ BECKET </s>
<s> ELEANOR </s>
<s> Fitzurse, that chart with the red line--thou sawest it--her bower </s>
<s> FITZURSE </s>
<s> Rosamund's </s>
<s> ELEANOR </s>
<s> Ay--there lies the secret of her whereabouts, and the King gave it to his Chancellor </s>
<s> FlTZURSE </s>
<s> To this son of a London merchant--how your Grace must hate him </s>
<s> ELEANOR </s>
<s> Hate him </s>
<s> as brave a Soldier as Henry and a goodlier man: but thou-- dost thou love this Chancellor, that thou hast sworn a voluntary allegiance to him </s>
<s> FlTZURSE </s>
<s> Not for my love toward him, but because he had the love of the King </s>
<s> How should a baron love a beggar on horseback, with the retinue of three kings behind him, outroyalling royalty </s>
<s> Besides, he holp the King to break down our castles, for the which I hate him </s>
<s> ELEANOR </s>
<s> For the which I honour him </s>
<s> Statesman not Churchman he </s>
<s> A great and sound policy that: I could embrace him for it: you could not see the King for the kinglings </s>
<s> FlTZURSE </s>
<s> Ay, but he speaks to a noble as tho' he were a churl, and to a churl as if he were a noble </s>
<s> ELEANOR </s>
<s> Pride of the plebeian </s>
<s> FlTZURSE </s>
<s> And this plebeian like to be Archbishop </s>
<s> ELEANOR </s>
<s> True, and I have an inherited loathing of these black sheep of the Papacy </s>
<s> Archbishop </s>
<s> I can see further into a man than our hot-headed Henry, and if there ever come feud between Church and Crown, and I do not then charm this secret out of our loyal Thomas, I am not Eleanor </s>
<s> FlTZURSE </s>
<s> Last night I followed a woman in the city here </s>
<s> Her face was veiled, but the back methought was Rosamund--his paramour, thy rival </s>
<s> I can feel for thee </s>
<s> ELEANOR </s>
<s> Thou feel for me!--paramour--rival </s>
<s> King Louis had no paramours, and I loved him none the more </s>
<s> Henry had many, and I loved him none the less--now neither more nor less--not at all; the cup's empty </s>
<s> I would she were but his paramour, for men tire of their fancies; but I fear this one fancy hath taken root, and borne blossom too, and she, whom the King loves indeed, is a power in the State </s>
<s> Rival!--ay, and when the King passes, there may come a crash and embroilment as in Stephen's time; and her children--canst thou not--that secret matter which would heat the King against thee (_whispers him and he starts_) </s>
<s> Nay, that is safe with me as with thyself: but canst thou not--thou art drowned in debt--thou shalt have our love, our silence, and our gold--canst thou not--if thou light upon her--free me from her </s>
<s> FITZURSE </s>
<s> Well, Madam, I have loved her in my time </s>
<s> ELEANOR </s>
<s> No, my bear, thou hast not </s>
<s> My Courts of Love would have held thee guiltless of love--the fine attractions and repulses, the delicacies, the subtleties </s>
<s> FITZURSE </s>
<s> Madam, I loved according to the main purpose and intent of nature </s>
<s> ELEANOR </s>
<s> I warrant thee </s>
<s> thou wouldst hug thy Cupid till his ribs cracked-- enough of this </s>
<s> Follow me this Rosamund day and night, whithersoever she goes; track her, if thou canst, even into the King's lodging, that I may (_clenches her fist_)--may at least have my cry against him and her,--and thou in thy way shouldst be jealous of the King, for thou in thy way didst once, what shall I call it, affect her thine own self </s>
<s> FITZURSE </s>
<s> Ay, but the young colt winced and whinnied and flung up her heels; and then the King came honeying about her, and this Becket, her father's friend, like enough staved us from her </s>
<s> ELEANOR </s>
<s> Us </s>
<s> FITZURSE </s>
<s> Yea, by the Blessed Virgin </s>
<s> There were more than I buzzing round the blossom--De Tracy--even that flint De Brito </s>
<s> ELEANOR </s>
<s> Carry her off among you; run in upon her and devour her, one and all of you; make her as hateful to herself and to the King, as she is to me </s>
<s> FITZURSE </s>
<s> I and all would be glad to wreak our spite on the rose-faced minion of the King, and bring her to the level of the dust, so that the King-- ELEANOR </s>
<s> Let her eat it like the serpent, and be driven out of her paradise </s>
<s> ACT ONE </s>
<s> SCENE I.--BECKET'S _House in London </s>
<s> Chamber barely furnished_ </s>
<s> BECKET _unrobing_ </s>
<s> HERBERT OF BOSHAM _and_ SERVANT </s>
<s> SERVANT </s>
<s> Shall I not help your lordship to your rest </s>
<s> BECKET </s>
<s> Friend, am I so much better than thyself That thou shouldst help me </s>
<s> Thou art wearied out With this day's work, get thee to thine own bed </s>
<s> Leave me with Herbert, friend </s>
<s> [_Exit_ SERVANT </s>
<s> Help me off, Herbert, with this--and this </s>
<s> HERBERT </s>
<s> Was not the people's blessing as we past Heart-comfort and a balsam to thy blood </s>
<s> BECKET </s>
<s> The people know their Church a tower of strength, A bulwark against Throne and Baronage </s>
<s> Too heavy for me, this; off with it, Herbert </s>
<s> HERBERT </s>
<s> Is it so much heavier than thy Chancellor's robe </s>
<s> BECKET </s>
<s> No; but the Chancellor's and the Archbishop's Together more than mortal man can bear </s>
<s> HERBERT </s>

<s> SCENE III.--_The Hall in Northampton Castle_ </s>

<s> JOHN OF OXFORD </s>

<s> No </s>
<s> JOHN OF OXFORD </s>

<s> And that I cannot sign: for that would make Our island-Church a schism from Christendom, And weight down all free choice beneath the throne </s>

<s> [_Sits on his throne_ </s>
<s> Barons and bishops of our realm of England, After the nineteen winters of King Stephen-- A reign which was no reign, when none could sit By his own hearth in peace; when murder common As nature's death, like Egypt's plague, had fill'd All things with blood; when every doorway blush'd, Dash'd red with that unhallow'd passover; When every baron ground his blade in blood; The household dough was kneaded up with blood; The millwheel turn'd in blood; the wholesome plow Lay rusting in the furrow's yellow weeds, Till famine dwarft the race--I came, your King </s>
<s> Nor dwelt alone, like a soft lord of the East, In mine own hall, and sucking thro' fools' ears The flatteries of corruption--went abroad Thro' all my counties, spied my people's ways; Yea, heard the churl against the baron--yea, And did him justice; sat in mine own courts Judging my judges, that had found a King Who ranged confusions, made the twilight day, And struck a shape from out the vague, and law From madness </s>
<s> And the event--our fallows till'd, Much corn, repeopled towns, a realm again </s>
<s> So far my course, albeit not glassy-smooth, Had prosper'd in the main, but suddenly Jarr'd on this rock </s>
<s> A cleric violated The daughter of his host, and murder'd him </s>
<s> Bishops--York, London, Chichester, Westminster-- Ye haled this tonsured devil into your courts; But since your canon will not let you take Life for a life, ye but degraded him Where I had hang'd him </s>
<s> What doth hard murder care For degradation </s>
<s> and that made me muse, Being bounden by my coronation oath To do men justice </s>
<s> Look to it, your own selves </s>
<s> Say that a cleric murder'd an archbishop, What could ye do </s>

<s> Call in the poor from the streets, and let them feast </s>
<s> HERBERT </s>
<s> That is the parable of our blessed Lord </s>
<s> BECKET </s>
<s> And why should not the parable of our blessed Lord be acted again </s>
<s> Call in the poor </s>
<s> The Church is ever at variance with the kings, and ever at one with the poor </s>
<s> I marked a group of lazars in the marketplace--half-rag, half-sore--beggars, poor rogues (Heaven bless 'em) who never saw nor dreamed of such a banquet </s>
<s> I will amaze them </s>
<s> Call them in, I say </s>
<s> They shall henceforward be my earls and barons-- our lords and masters in Christ Jesus </s>
<s> [_Exit_ HERBERT </s>
<s> If the King hold his purpose, I am myself a beggar </s>
<s> Forty thousand marks </s>
<s> forty thousand devils--and these craven bishops </s>
<s> _A_ POOR MAN _(entering) with his dog_ </s>
<s> My lord Archbishop, may I come in with my poor friend, my dog </s>

<s> The King's courts would use thee worse than thy dog--they are too bloody </s>
<s> Were the Church king, it would be otherwise </s>
<s> Poor beast </s>
<s> poor beast </s>
<s> set him down </s>
<s> I will bind up his wounds with my napkin </s>
<s> Give him a bone, give him a bone </s>
<s> Who misuses a dog would misuse a child--they cannot speak for themselves </s>
<s> Past help </s>
<s> his paws are past help </s>
<s> God help him </s>
<s> _Enter the_ BEGGARS _(and seat themselves at the Tables)_ </s>
<s> BECKET _and_ HERBERT _wait upon them_ </s>
<s> 1ST BEGGAR </s>

<s> Peace </s>

<s> Peace </s>

<s> ACT II </s>
<s> SCENE I.--ROSAMUND'S _Bower </s>
<s> A Garden of Flowers </s>
<s> In the midst a bank of wild-flowers with a bench before it_ </s>
<s> _Voices heard singing among the trees_ </s>
<s> _Duet_ </s>
<s> 1 </s>
<s> Is it the wind of the dawn that I hear in the pine overhead </s>
<s> 2 </s>
<s> No; but the voice of the deep as it hollows the cliffs of the land </s>
<s> 1 </s>
<s> Is there a voice coming up with the voice of the deep from the strand, One coming up with a song in the flush of the glimmering red </s>
<s> 2 </s>
<s> Love that is born of the deep coming up with the sun from the sea </s>
<s> 1 </s>
<s> Love that can shape or can shatter a life till the life shall have fled </s>
<s> 2 </s>
<s> Nay, let us welcome him, Love that can lift up a life from the dead </s>
<s> 1 </s>
<s> Keep him away from the lone little isle </s>
<s> Let us be, let us be </s>
<s> 2 </s>
<s> Nay, let him make it his own, let him reign in it--he, it is he, Love that is born of the deep coming up with the sun from the sea </s>
<s> _Enter_ HENRY _and_ ROSAMUND </s>
<s> ROSAMUND </s>
<s> Be friends with him again--I do beseech thee </s>
<s> HENRY </s>
<s> With Becket </s>
<s> I have but one hour with thee-- Sceptre and crozier clashing, and the mitre Grappling the crown--and when I flee from this For a gasp of freer air, a breathing-while To rest upon thy bosom and forget him-- Why thou, my bird, thou pipest Becket, Becket-- Yea, thou my golden dream of Love's own bower, Must be the nightmare breaking on my peace With 'Becket' </s>
<s> ROSAMUND </s>
<s> O my life's life, not to smile Is all but death to me </s>
<s> My sun, no cloud </s>
<s> Let there not be one frown in this one hour </s>
<s> Out of the many thine, let this be mine </s>
<s> Look rather thou all-royal as when first I met thee </s>
<s> HENRY </s>
<s> Where was that </s>
<s> ROSAMUND </s>
<s> Forgetting that Forgets me too </s>
<s> HENRY </s>
<s> Nay, I remember it well </s>
<s> There on the moors </s>
<s> ROSAMUND </s>
<s> And in a narrow path </s>

<s> And from that height something was said to me I knew not what </s>
<s> HENRY </s>
<s> I ask'd the way </s>
<s> ROSAMUND </s>
<s> I think so </s>

<s> HENRY </s>

<s> The rosebud of my rose!-- Well, well, no more of _him_--I have sent his folk, His kin, all his belongings, overseas; Age, orphans, and babe-breasting mothers--all By hundreds to him--there to beg, starve, die-- So that the fool King Louis feed them not </s>
<s> The man shall feel that I can strike him yet </s>
<s> ROSAMUND </s>
<s> Babes, orphans, mothers </s>
<s> is that royal, Sire </s>
<s> HENRY </s>
<s> And I have been as royal with the Church </s>
<s> He shelter'd in the Abbey of Pontigny </s>
<s> There wore his time studying the canon law To work it against me </s>
<s> But since he cursed My friends at Veselay, I have let them know, That if they keep him longer as their guest, I scatter all their cowls to all the hells </s>
<s> ROSAMUND </s>
<s> And is that altogether royal </s>
<s> HENRY </s>
<s> Traitress </s>
<s> ROSAMUND </s>
<s> A faithful traitress to thy royal fame </s>
<s> HENRY </s>
<s> Fame </s>
<s> what care I for fame </s>

<s> Fame of to-day is infamy to-morrow; Infamy of to-day is fame to-morrow; And round and round again </s>
<s> What matters </s>
<s> Royal--I mean to leave the royalty of my crown Unlessen'd to mine heirs </s>
<s> ROSAMUND </s>
<s> Still--thy fame too: I say that should be royal </s>
<s> HENRY </s>
<s> And I say, I care not for thy saying </s>

<s> HENRY </s>

<s> no need!.. </s>

<s> SCENE II.--_Montmirail </s>
<s> 'The Meeting of the Kings'._ JOHN OF OXFORD _and_ HENRY </s>

<s> You have not crown'd young Henry yet, my liege </s>

<s> HENRY </s>

<s> and Becket Becket should crown him were he crown'd at all: But, since we would be lord of our own manor, This Canterbury, like a wounded deer, Has fled our presence and our feeding-grounds </s>

<s> I must patch up a peace-- A piece in this long-tugged at, threadbare-worn Quarrel of Crown and Church--to rend again </s>

<s> _Enter_ WALTER MAP </s>
<s> WALTER MAP </s>
<s> Pity, my lord, that you have quenched the warmth of France toward you, tho' His Holiness, after much smouldering and smoking, be kindled again upon your quarter </s>

<s> Ay, if he do not end in smoke again </s>
<s> WALTER MAP </s>
<s> My lord, the fire, when first kindled, said to the smoke, 'Go up, my son, straight to Heaven' </s>
<s> And the smoke said, 'I go;' but anon the North-east took and turned him South-west, then the South-west turned him North-east, and so of the other winds; but it was in him to go up straight if the time had been quieter </s>
<s> Your lordship affects the unwavering perpendicular; but His Holiness, pushed one way by the Empire and another by England, if he move at all, Heaven stay him, is fain to diagonalise </s>
<s> HERBERT </s>
<s> Diagonalise </s>
<s> thou art a word-monger </s>

<s> WALTER MAP </s>

<s> BECKET </s>
<s> Ay, if the jest be so done that the people Delight to wallow in the grossness of it, Till Truth herself be shamed of her defender </s>

<s> WALTER MAP </s>
<s> Is that my case </s>
<s> so if the city be sick, and I cannot call the kennel sweet, your lordship would suspend me from verse-writing, as you suspended yourself after subwriting to the customs </s>

<s> I pray God pardon mine infirmity </s>
<s> WALTER MAP </s>
<s> Nay, my lord, take heart; for tho' you suspended yourself, the Pope let you down again; and tho' you suspend Foliot or another, the Pope will not leave them in suspense, for the Pope himself is always in suspense, like Mahound's coffin hung between heaven and earth--always in suspense, like the scales, till the weight of Germany or the gold of England brings one of them down to the dust--always in suspense, like the tail of the horologe--to and fro--tick-tack--we make the time, we keep the time, ay, and we serve the time; for I have heard say that if you boxed the Pope's ears with a purse, you might stagger him, but he would pocket the purse </s>

<s> ACT III </s>
<s> SCENE I.--_The Bower_ </s>

<s> _Enter_ MARGERY </s>
<s> I ha' been but a week here and I ha' seen what I ha' seen, for to be sure it's no more than a week since our old Father Philip that has confessed our mother for twenty years, and she was hard put to it, and to speak truth, nigh at the end of our last crust, and that mouldy, and she cried out on him to put me forth in the world and to make me a woman of the world, and to win my own bread, whereupon he asked our mother if I could keep a quiet tongue i' my head, and not speak till I was spoke to, and I answered for myself that I never spoke more than was needed, and he told me he would advance me to the service of a great lady, and took me ever so far away, and gave me a great pat o' the cheek for a pretty wench, and said it was a pity to blindfold such eyes as mine, and such to be sure they be, but he blinded 'em for all that, and so brought me no-hows as I may say, and the more shame to him after his promise, into a garden and not into the world, and bad me whatever I saw not to speak one word, an' it 'ud be well for me in the end, for there were great ones who would look after me, and to be sure I ha' seen great ones to-day--and then not to speak one word, for that's the rule o' the garden, tho' to be sure if I had been Eve i' the garden I shouldn't ha' minded the apple, for what's an apple, you know, save to a child, and I'm no child, but more a woman o the world than my lady here, and I ha' seen what I ha' seen--tho' to be sure if I hadn't minded it we should all on us ha' had to go, bless the Saints, wi' bare backs, but the backs 'ud ha' countenanced one another, and belike it 'ud ha' been always summer, and anyhow I am as well-shaped as my lady here, and I ha' seen what I ha' seen, and what's the good of my talking to myself, for here comes my lady (_enter_ ROSAMUND), and, my lady, tho' I shouldn't speak one word, I wish you joy o' the King's brother </s>
<s> ROSAMUND </s>
<s> What is it you mean </s>
<s> MARGERY </s>
<s> I mean your goodman, your husband, my lady, for I saw your ladyship a-parting wi' him even now i' the coppice, when I was a-getting o' bluebells for your ladyship's nose to smell on--and I ha' seen the King once at Oxford, and he's as like the King as fingernail to fingernail, and I thought at first it was the King, only you know the King's married, for King Louis-- ROSAMUND </s>
<s> Married </s>

<s> MARGERY </s>

<s> SCENE III.--_Traitor's Meadow at Fréteval </s>

<s> _Enter_ KING HENRY _and_ WALTER MAP </s>
<s> HENRY </s>
<s> We have had so many hours together, Thomas, So many happy hours alone together, That I would speak with you once more alone </s>

<s> HERBERT </s>

<s> HERBERT </s>
<s> And feel it too </s>
<s> WALTER MAP </s>
<s> And see you yon side-beam that is forced from under it, and sets the church-tower over there all a-hell-fire as it were </s>
<s> HERBERT </s>
<s> Ay </s>
<s> WALTER MAP </s>
<s> It is this black, bell-silencing, anti-marrying, burial-hindering interdict that hath squeezed out this side-smile upon Canterbury, whereof may come conflagration </s>
<s> Were I Thomas, I wouldn't trust it </s>
<s> Sudden change is a house on sand; and tho' I count Henry honest enough, yet when fear creeps in at the front, honesty steals out at the back, and the King at last is fairly scared by this cloud--this interdict </s>
<s> I have been more for the King than the Church in this matter--yea, even for the sake of the Church: for, truly, as the case stood, you had safelier have slain an archbishop than a she-goat: but our recoverer and upholder of customs hath in this crowning of young Henry by York and London so violated the immemorial usage of the Church, that, like the gravedigger's child I have heard of, trying to ring the bell, he hath half-hanged himself in the rope of the Church, or rather pulled all the Church with the Holy Father astride of it down upon his own head </s>
<s> HERBERT </s>
<s> Were you there </s>
<s> WALTER MAP </s>
<s> In the church rope?--no </s>
<s> I was at the crowning, for I have pleasure in the pleasure of crowds, and to read the faces of men at a great show </s>
<s> HERBERT </s>
<s> And how did Roger of York comport himself </s>
<s> WALTER MAP </s>
<s> As magnificently and archiepiscopally as our Thomas would have done: only there was a dare-devil in his eye--I should say a dare-Becket </s>
<s> He thought less of two kings than of one Roger the king of the occasion </s>
<s> Foliot is the holier man, perhaps the better </s>
<s> Once or twice there ran a twitch across his face as who should say what's to follow </s>
<s> but Salisbury was a calf cowed by Mother Church, and every now and then glancing about him like a thief at night when he hears a door open in the house and thinks 'the master' </s>
<s> HERBERT </s>
<s> And the father-king </s>
<s> WALTER MAP </s>
<s> The father's eye was so tender it would have called a goose off the green, and once he strove to hide his face, like the Greek king when his daughter was sacrificed, but he thought better of it: it was but the sacrifice of a kingdom to his son, a smaller matter; but as to the young crownling himself, he looked so malapert in the eyes, that had I fathered him I had given him more of the rod than the sceptre </s>
<s> Then followed the thunder of the captains and the shouting, and so we came on to the banquet, from whence there puffed out such an incense of unctuosity into the nostrils of our Gods of Church and State, that Lucullus or Apicius might have sniffed it in their Hades of heathenism, so that the smell of their own roast had not come across it-- HERBERT </s>
<s> Map, tho' you make your butt too big, you overshoot it </s>
<s> WALTER MAP </s>
<s> --For as to the fish, they de-miracled the miraculous draught, and might have sunk a navy-- HERBERT </s>
<s> There again, Goliasing and Goliathising </s>
<s> WALTER MAP </s>
<s> --And as for the flesh at table, a whole Peter's sheet, with all manner of game, and four-footed things, and fowls-- HERBERT </s>
<s> And all manner of creeping things too </s>
<s> WALTER MAP </s>
<s> --Well, there were Abbots--but they did not bring their women; and so we were dull enough at first, but in the end we flourished out into a merriment; for the old King would act servitor and hand a dish to his son; whereupon my Lord of York--his fine-cut face bowing and beaming with all that courtesy which hath less loyalty in it than the backward scrape of the clown's heel--'great honour,' says he, 'from the King's self to the King's son' </s>
<s> Did you hear the young King's quip </s>
<s> HERBERT </s>
<s> No, what was it </s>
<s> WALTER MAP </s>
<s> Glancing at the days when his father was only Earl of Anjou, he answered:--'Should not an earl's son wait on a king's son' </s>
<s> And when the cold corners of the King's mouth began to thaw, there was a great motion of laughter among us, part real, part childlike, to be freed from the dulness--part royal, for King and kingling both laughed, and so we could not but laugh, as by a royal necessity--part childlike again--when we felt we had laughed too long and could not stay ourselves--many midriff-shaken even to tears, as springs gush out after earthquakes--but from those, as I said before, there may come a conflagration--tho', to keep the figure moist and make it hold water, I should say rather, the lacrymation of a lamentation; but look if Thomas have not flung himself at the King's feet </s>
<s> They have made it up again--for the moment </s>
<s> HERBERT </s>
<s> Thanks to the blessed Magdalen, whose day it is </s>
<s> _Re-enter_ HENRY _and_ BECKET </s>

<s> ACT V </s>

<s> Let all that be </s>

<s> SCENE II.--_A Room in Canterbury Monastery_ </s>
<s> BECKET _and_ JOHN OF SALISBURY </s>
<s> BECKET </s>
<s> York said so </s>

<s> Yes: a man may take good counsel Ev'n from his foe </s>

<s> Can the King de-anathematise this York </s>
<s> JOHN OF SALISBURY </s>
<s> Thomas, I would thou hadst return'd to England, Like some wise prince of this world from his wars, With more of olive-branch and amnesty For foes at home--thou hast raised the world against thee </s>
<s> BECKET </s>
<s> Why, John, my kingdom is not of this world </s>
<s> JOHN OF SALISBURY </s>
<s> If it were more of this world it might be More of the next </s>
<s> A policy of wise pardon Wins here as well as there </s>
<s> To bless thine enemies-- BECKET </s>
<s> Ay, mine, not Heaven's </s>
<s> JOHN OF SALISBURY </s>
<s> And may there not be something Of this world's leaven in thee too, when crying On Holy Church to thunder out her rights And thine own wrong so pitilessly </s>
<s> Ah, Thomas, The lightnings that we think are only Heaven's Flash sometimes out of earth against the heavens </s>
<s> The soldier, when he lets his whole self go Lost in the common good, the common wrong, Strikes truest ev'n for his own self </s>
<s> I crave Thy pardon--I have still thy leave to speak </s>
<s> Thou hast waged God's war against the King; and yet We are self-uncertain creatures, and we may, Yea, even when we know not, mix our spites And private hates with our defence of Heaven </s>
<s> [_Enter_ EDWARD GRIM </s>
<s> BECKET </s>
<s> Thou art but yesterday from Cambridge, Grim; What say ye there of Becket </s>

<s> York against Canterbury, York against God </s>

<s> I met a robber once, I told him I was bound to see the Archbishop; 'Pass on,' he said, and in thy name I pass'd From house to house </s>
<s> In one a son stone-blind Sat by his mother's hearth: he had gone too far Into the King's own woods; and the poor mother, Soon as she learnt I was a friend of thine, Cried out against the cruelty of the King </s>

<s> More gain than loss; for of your wives you shall Find one a slut whose fairest linen seems Foul as her dust-cloth, if she used it--one So charged with tongue, that every thread of thought Is broken ere it joins--a shrew to boot, Whose evil song far on into the night Thrills to the topmost tile--no hope but death; One slow, fat, white, a burthen of the hearth; And one that being thwarted ever swoons And weeps herself into the place of power; And one an _uxor pauperis Ibyci_ </s>

<s> SCENE III.--_North Transept of Canterbury Cathedral </s>
<s> On the right hand a flight of steps leading to the Choir, another flight on the left, leading to the North Aisle </s>
<s> Winter afternoon slowly darkening </s>
<s> Low thunder now and then of an approaching storm_ </s>
<s> MONKS _heard chanting the service_ </s>
<s> ROSAMUND _kneeling_ </s>
<s> ROSAMUND </s>
<s> O blessed saint, O glorious Benedict,-- These arm'd men in the city, these fierce faces-- Thy holy follower founded Canterbury-- Save that dear head which now is Canterbury, Save him, he saved my life, he saved my child, Save him, his blood would darken Henry's name; Save him till all as saintly as thyself He miss the searching flame of purgatory, And pass at once perfect to Paradise </s>

<s> ACT I </s>
<s> SCENE I.--_Distant View of a City of Galatia_ </s>
<s> As the curtain rises, Priestesses are heard singing in the Temple </s>
<s> Boy discovered on a pathway among Rocks, picking grapes </s>
<s> A party of Roman Soldiers, guarding a prisoner in chains, come down the pathway and exeunt </s>
<s> _Enter_ SYNORIX (_looking round_) </s>
<s> _Singing ceases_ </s>
<s> SYNORIX </s>
<s> Pine, beech and plane, oak, walnut, apricot, Vine, cypress, poplar, myrtle, bowering in The city where she dwells </s>
<s> She past me here Three years ago when I was flying from My Tetrarchy to Rome </s>
<s> I almost touch'd her-- A maiden slowly moving on to music Among her maidens to this Temple--O Gods </s>
<s> She is my fate--else wherefore has my fate Brought me again to her own city?--married Since--married Sinnatus, the Tetrarch here-- But if he be conspirator, Rome will chain, Or slay him </s>
<s> I may trust to gain her then When I shall have my tetrarchy restored By Rome, our mistress, grateful that I show'd her The weakness and the dissonance of our clans, And how to crush them easily </s>
<s> Wretched race </s>
<s> And once I wish'd to scourge them to the bones </s>
<s> But in this narrow breathing-time of life Is vengeance for its own sake worth the while, If once our ends are gain'd </s>
<s> and now this cup-- I never felt such passion for a woman </s>
<s> [_Brings out a cup and scroll from under his cloak_ </s>
<s> What have I written to her </s>
<s> [_Reading the scroll_ </s>
<s> 'To the admired Gamma, wife of Sinnatus, the Tetrarch, one who years ago, himself an adorer of our great goddess, Artemis, beheld you afar off worshipping in her Temple, and loved you for it, sends you this cup rescued from the burning of one of her shrines in a city thro' which he past with the Roman army: it is the cup we use in our marriages </s>
<s> Receive it from one who cannot at present write himself other than 'A GALATIAN SERVING BY FORCE IN THE ROMAN LEGION' </s>
<s> [_Turns and looks up to Boy_ </s>
<s> Boy, dost thou know the house of Sinnatus </s>
<s> BOY </s>
<s> These grapes are for the house of Sinnatus-- Close to the Temple </s>
<s> SYNORIX </s>
<s> Yonder </s>
<s> BOY </s>
<s> Yes </s>
<s> SYNORIX (_aside_) </s>
<s> That I With all my range of women should yet shun To meet her face to face at once </s>
<s> My boy, [_Boy comes down rocks to him_ </s>
<s> Take thou this letter and this cup to Camma, The wife of Sinnatus </s>
<s> BOY </s>
<s> Going or gone to-day To hunt with Sinnatus </s>
<s> SYNORIX </s>
<s> That matters not </s>
<s> Take thou this cup and leave it at her doors </s>
<s> [_Gives the cup and scroll to the Boy_ </s>
<s> BOY </s>
<s> I will, my lord </s>
<s> [_Takes his basket of grapes and exit_ </s>
<s> _Enter_ ANTONIUS </s>
<s> ANTONIUS (_meeting the Boy as he goes out_) </s>
<s> Why, whither runs the boy </s>
<s> Is that the cup you rescued from the fire </s>
<s> SYNORIX </s>
<s> I send it to the wife of Sinnatus, One half besotted in religious rites </s>
<s> You come here with your soldiers to enforce The long-withholden tribute: you suspect This Sinnatus of playing patriotism, Which in your sense is treason </s>
<s> You have yet No proof against him: now this pious cup Is passport to their house, and open arms To him who gave it; and once there I warrant I worm thro' all their windings </s>
<s> ANTONIUS </s>
<s> If you prosper, Our Senate, wearied of their tetrarchies, Their quarrels with themselves, their spites at Rome, Is like enough to cancel them, and throne One king above them all, who shall be true To the Roman: and from what I heard in Rome, This tributary crown may fall to you </s>
<s> SYNORIX </s>
<s> The king, the crown </s>
<s> their talk in Rome </s>
<s> is it so </s>
<s> [ANTONIUS _nods_ </s>
<s> Well--I shall serve Galatia taking it, And save her from herself, and be to Rome More faithful than a Roman </s>
<s> [_Turns and sees_ CAMMA _coming_ </s>
<s> Stand aside, Stand aside; here she comes </s>

<s> Where is he, girl </s>
<s> MAID </s>

<s> CAMMA </s>
<s> The stag is there </s>
<s> MAID </s>
<s> Seen in the thicket at the bottom there But yester-even </s>

<s> Sinnatus' </s>

<s> Looking off stage_.] He comes, a rough, bluff, simple-looking fellow </s>
<s> If we may judge the kernel by the husk, Not one to keep a woman's fealty when Assailed by Craft and Love </s>

<s> I see no face that knows me </s>

<s> _Enter_ SINNATUS, HUNTSMEN _and hounds_ </s>

<s> Ay, ay, why not </s>

<s> SCENE II.--_A Room in the Tetrarch's House_ </s>
<s> Frescoed figures on the walls </s>
<s> Evening </s>

<s> No Sinnatus yet--and there the rising moon </s>
<s> [_Takes up a cithern and sits on couch </s>

<s> I thought I heard A footstep </s>
<s> No not yet </s>

<s> 'To the admired Camma,--beheld you afar off--loved you--sends you this cup--the cup we use in our marriages--cannot at present write himself other than 'A GALATIAN SERVING BY FORCE IN THE ROMAN LEGION' </s>
<s> Serving by force </s>
<s> Were there no boughs to hang on, Rivers to drown in </s>
<s> Serve by force </s>
<s> No force Could make me serve by force </s>
<s> SYNORIX </s>
<s> How then, my lord </s>
<s> The Roman is encampt without your city-- The force of Rome a thousand-fold our own </s>
<s> Must all Galatia hang or drown herself </s>

<s> Province </s>
<s> SYNORIX </s>
<s> Well, well, they call it so in Rome </s>
<s> SINNATUS (_angrily_) </s>
<s> Province </s>
<s> SYNORIX </s>
<s> A noble anger </s>
<s> but Antonius To-morrow will demand your tribute--you, Can you make war </s>
<s> Have you alliances </s>
<s> Bithynia, Pontus, Paphlagonia </s>
<s> We have had our leagues of old with Eastern kings </s>
<s> There is my hand--if such a league there be </s>
<s> What will you do </s>
<s> SINNATUS </s>
<s> Not set myself abroach And run my mind out to a random guest Who join'd me in the hunt </s>
<s> You saw my hounds True to the scent; and we have two-legg'd dogs Among us who can smell a true occasion, And when to bark and how </s>
<s> SYNORIX </s>
<s> My good Lord Sinnatus, I once was at the hunting of a lion </s>
<s> Roused by the clamour of the chase he woke, Came to the front of the wood--his monarch mane Bristled about his quick ears--he stood there Staring upon the hunter </s>
<s> A score of dogs Gnaw'd at his ankles: at the last he felt The trouble of his feet, put forth one paw, Slew four, and knew it not, and so remain'd Staring upon the hunter: and this Rome Will crush you if you wrestle with her; then Save for some slight report in her own Senate Scarce know what she has done </s>
<s> (_Aside_.) Would I could move him, Provoke him any way </s>
<s> (_Aloud_.) The Lady Camma, Wise I am sure as she is beautiful, Will close with me that to submit at once Is better than a wholly-hopeless war, Our gallant citizens murder'd all in vain, Son, husband, brother gash'd to death in vain, And the small state more cruelly trampled on Than had she never moved </s>
<s> CAMMA </s>
<s> Sir, I had once A boy who died a babe; but were he living And grown to man and Sinnatus will'd it, I Would set him in the front rank of the fight With scarce a pang </s>
<s> (_Rises_.) Sir, if a state submit At once, she may be blotted out at once And swallow'd in the conqueror's chronicle </s>
<s> Whereas in wars of freedom and defence The glory and grief of battle won or lost Solders a race together--yea--tho' they fail, The names of those who fought and fell are like A bank'd-up fire that flashes out again From century to century, and at last May lead them on to victory--I hope so-- Like phantoms of the Gods </s>
<s> SINNATUS </s>
<s> Well spoken, wife </s>
<s> SYNORIX (_bowing_) </s>
<s> Madam, so well I yield </s>
<s> SINNATUS </s>

<s> ACT II SCENE.--_Interior of the Temple of Artemis_ </s>
<s> Small gold gates on platform in front of the veil before the colossal statue of the Goddess, and in the centre of the Temple a tripod altar, on which is a lighted lamp </s>
<s> Lamps (lighted) suspended between each pillar </s>
<s> Tripods, vases, garlands of flowers, etc, about stage </s>
<s> Altar at back close to Goddess, with two cups </s>

<s> Priestesses decorating the Temple </s>

<s> Good </s>
<s> mine own dagger driven by Synorix found All good in the true heart of Sinnatus, And quench'd it there for ever </s>

<s> We cannot fight imperial Rome, But he and I are both Galatian-born, And tributary sovereigns, he and I Might teach this Rome--from knowledge of our people-- Where to lay on her tribute--heavily here And lightly there </s>

<s> Most like it was the Roman soldier shouted </s>

<s> LADY GIOVANNA </s>

<s> COUNT (_impetuously_) </s>
<s> Why then the dying of my noble bird Hath served me better than her living--then [_Takes diamonds from table_ </s>

<s> The purpose of my being is accomplish'd, And I am happy </s>
<s> LADY GIOVANNA </s>
<s> And I too, Federigo </s>
<s> THE PROMISE OF MAY 'A surface man of theories, true to none' </s>
<s> _DRAMATIS PERSONAE </s>

<s> THE PROMISE OF MAY ACT I </s>
<s> SCENE.--_Before Farmhouse_ </s>
<s> Farming Men and Women </s>
<s> Farming Men carrying forms, &c., Women carrying baskets of knives and forks, &c </s>
<s> 1ST FARMING MAN </s>
<s> Be thou a-gawin' to the long barn </s>
<s> 2ND FARMING MAN </s>
<s> Ay, to be sewer </s>
<s> Be thou </s>
<s> 1ST FARMING MAN </s>
<s> Why, o' coorse, fur it be the owd man's birthdaäy </s>
<s> He be heighty this very daäy, and 'e telled all on us to be i' the long barn by one o'clock, fur he'll gie us a big dinner, and haäfe th' parish'll be theer, an' Miss Dora, an' Miss Eva, an' all </s>

<s> (_Pointing to house_.) <s> This author, with his charm of simple style And close dialectic, all but proving man An automatic series of sensations, Has often numb'd me into apathy Against the unpleasant jolts of this rough road That breaks off short into the abysses--made me A Quietist taking all things easily </s>

<s> EDGAR </s>
<s> Jealous of me with Eva </s>
<s> Is it so </s>
<s> Well, tho' I grudge the pretty jewel, that I Have worn, to such a clod, yet that might be The best way out of it, if the child could keep Her counsel </s>
<s> I am sure I wish her happy </s>
<s> But I must free myself from this entanglement </s>
<s> I have all my life before me--so has she-- Give her a month or two, and her affections Will flower toward the light in some new face </s>

<s> She will urge marriage on me </s>
<s> I hate tears </s>
<s> Marriage is but an old tradition </s>
<s> I hate Traditions, ever since my narrow father, After my frolic with his tenant's girl, Made younger elder son, violated the whole Tradition of our land, and left his heir, Born, happily, with some sense of art, to live By brush and pencil </s>
<s> By and by, when Thought Comes down among the crowd, and man perceives that The lost gleam of an after-life but leaves him A beast of prey in the dark, why then the crowd May wreak my wrongs upon my wrongers </s>
<s> Marriage </s>
<s> That fine, fat, hook-nosed uncle of mine, old Harold, Who leaves me all his land at Littlechester, He, too, would oust me from his will, if I Made such a marriage </s>
<s> And marriage in itself-- The storm is hard at hand will sweep away Thrones, churches, ranks, traditions, customs, marriage One of the feeblest </s>
<s> Then the man, the woman, Following their best affinities, will each Bid their old bond farewell with smiles, not tears; Good wishes, not reproaches; with no fear Of the world's gossiping clamour, and no need Of veiling their desires </s>
<s> Conventionalism, Who shrieks by day at what she does by night, Would call this vice; but one time's vice may be The virtue of another; and Vice and Virtue Are but two masks of self; and what hereafter Shall mark out Vice from Virtue in the gulf Of never-dawning darkness </s>

<s> More like the picture Of Christian in my 'Pilgrim's Progress' here, Bow'd to the dust beneath the burthen of sin </s>

<s> Sin </s>
<s> What sin </s>
<s> DORA </s>
<s> Not his own </s>
<s> HAROLD </s>
<s> That nursery-tale Still read, then </s>
<s> DORA </s>

<s> Carters and shepherds </s>
<s> DORA </s>
<s> Scorn </s>
<s> I hate scorn </s>
<s> A soul with no religion-- My mother used to say that such a one Was without rudder, anchor, compass--might be Blown everyway with every gust and wreck On any rock; and tho' you are good and gentle, Yet if thro' any want-- HAROLD </s>
<s> Of this religion </s>
<s> Child, read a little history, you will find The common brotherhood of man has been Wrong'd by the cruelties of his religions More than could ever have happen'd thro' the want Of any or all of them </s>
<s> DORA </s>
<s> --But, O dear friend, If thro' the want of any--I mean the true one-- And pardon me for saying it--you should ever Be tempted into doing what might seem Not altogether worthy of you, I think That I should break my heart, for you have taught me To love you </s>
<s> HAROLD </s>
<s> What is this </s>
<s> some one been stirring Against me </s>
<s> he, your rustic amourist, The polish'd Damon of your pastoral here, This Dobson of your idyll </s>
<s> DORA </s>
<s> No, Sir, no </s>
<s> Did you not tell me he was crazed with jealousy, Had threaten'd ev'n your life, and would say anything </s>
<s> Did _I_ not promise not to listen to him, Not ev'n to see the man </s>
<s> HAROLD </s>
<s> Good; then what is it That makes you talk so dolefully </s>
<s> DORA </s>
<s> I told you-- My father </s>
<s> Well, indeed, a friend just now, One that has been much wrong'd, whose griefs are mine, Was warning me that if a gentleman Should wed a farmer's daughter, he would be Sooner or later shamed of her among The ladies, born his equals </s>
<s> HAROLD </s>
<s> More fool he </s>
<s> What I that have been call'd a Socialist, A Communist, a Nihilist--what you will!-- DORA </s>
<s> What are all these </s>
<s> HAROLD </s>
<s> Utopian idiotcies </s>
<s> They did not last three Junes </s>
<s> Such rampant weeds Strangle each other, die, and make the soil For Caesars, Cromwells, and Napoleons To root their power in </s>
<s> I have freed myself From all such dreams, and some will say because I have inherited my Uncle </s>
<s> Let them </s>
<s> But--shamed of you, my Empress </s>
<s> I should prize The pearl of Beauty, 'even if I found it Dark with the soot of slums </s>
<s> DORA </s>
<s> But I can tell you, We Steers are of old blood, tho' we be fallen </s>
<s> See there our shield </s>
<s> (_Pointing to arms on mantelpiece_.) For I have heard the Steers Had land in Saxon times; and your own name Of Harold sounds so English and so old I am sure you must be proud of it </s>
<s> HAROLD </s>
<s> Not I </s>
<s> As yet I scarcely feel it mine </s>
<s> I took it For some three thousand acres </s>
<s> I have land now And wealth, and lay both at your feet </s>
<s> DORA </s>
<s> And _what_ was Your name before </s>
<s> HAROLD </s>
<s> Come, come, my girl, enough Of this strange talk </s>
<s> I love you and you me </s>
<s> True, I have held opinions, hold some still, Which you would scarce approve of: for all that, I am a man not prone to jealousies, Caprices, humours, moods; but very ready To make allowances, and mighty slow To feel offences </s>
<s> Nay, I do believe I could forgive--well, almost anything-- And that more freely than your formal priest, Because I know more fully than _he_ can What poor earthworms are all and each of us, Here crawling in this boundless Nature </s>
<s> Dora, If marriage ever brought a woman happiness I doubt not I can make you happy </s>
<s> DORA </s>
<s> You make me Happy already </s>
<s> HAROLD </s>
<s> And I never said As much before to any woman living </s>
<s> DORA </s>
<s> No </s>
<s> HAROLD </s>
<s> No </s>
<s> by this true kiss, _you_ are the first I ever have loved truly </s>

<s> no, not they </s>

<s> _Enter_ MILLY </s>

<s> DORA (_to_ DOBSON) </s>
<s> Peace, let him be: it is the chamber of Death </s>
<s> Sir, you are tenfold more a gentleman, A hundred times more worth a woman's love, Than this, this--but I waste no words upon him: His wickedness is like my wretchedness-- Beyond all language </s>
<s> (_To_ HAROLD.) You--you see her there </s>
<s> Only fifteen when first you came on her, And then the sweetest flower of all the wolds, So lovely in the promise of her May, So winsome in her grace and gaiety, So loved by all the village people here, So happy in herself and in her home-- DOBSON (_agitated_) </s>

<s> ha' done </s>

<s> DORA </s>
<s> A child, and all as trustful as a child </s>
<s> Five years of shame and suffering broke the heart That only beat for you; and he, the father, Thro' that dishonour which you brought upon us, Has lost his health, his eyesight, even his mind </s>
<s> HAROLD (_covering his face_) </s>
<s> Enough </s>
